This file contains the 300 dpi bitmap fonts for the Times font family. The bitmap
fonts are required only if the PostScript printer dirver PSPrinter is used in
Oberon for Windows. To install the font files, start Oberon for Windows, open this
text file with Edit.Open and change the current directory to be the fonts directory
(e.g. c:\oberon\fonts if your Oberon for Windows is installed in c:\oberon.)
Then, execute the command AsciiCoder.DecodeFiles written below to unpack
the font files.

AsciiCoder.DecodeFiles % Times.Lm3.Fnt Times8.Pr3.Fnt Times8b.Pr3.Fnt Times8i.Pr3.Fnt Times10.Pr3.Fnt Times10b.Pr3.Fnt Times10i.Pr3.Fnt Times12.Pr3.Fnt Times12b.Pr3.Fnt Times12i.Pr3.Fnt Times14.Pr3.Fnt Times14b.Pr3.Fnt Times14i.Pr3.Fnt Times16.Pr3.Fnt Times16b.Pr3.Fnt Times16i.Pr3.Fnt Times20.Pr3.Fnt Times20b.Pr3.Fnt Times20i.Pr3.Fnt Times24.Pr3.Fnt Times24b.Pr3.Fnt Times24i.Pr3.Fnt ~
